    47	/// Logical representation of a user-defined [aggregate function] (UDAF).
    48	///
    49	/// An aggregate function combines the values from multiple input rows
    50	/// into a single output "aggregate" (summary) row. It is different
    51	/// from a scalar function because it is stateful across batches. User
    52	/// defined aggregate functions can be used as normal SQL aggregate
    53	/// functions (`GROUP BY` clause) as well as window functions (`OVER`
    54	/// clause).
    55	///
    56	/// `AggregateUDF` provides DataFusion the information needed to plan and call
    57	/// aggregate functions, including name, type information, and a factory
    58	/// function to create an [`Accumulator`] instance, to perform the actual
    59	/// aggregation.
    60	///
    61	/// For more information, please see [the examples]:
    62	///
    63	/// 1. For simple use cases, use [`create_udaf`] (examples in [`simple_udaf.rs`]).
    64	///
    65	/// 2. For advanced use cases, use [`AggregateUDFImpl`] which provides full API
    66	///    access (examples in [`advanced_udaf.rs`]).
    67	///
    68	/// # API Note
    69	/// This is a separate struct from `AggregateUDFImpl` to maintain backwards
    70	/// compatibility with the older API.
    71	///
    72	/// [the examples]: https://github.com/apache/datafusion/tree/main/datafusion-examples#single-process
    73	/// [aggregate function]: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aggregate_function
    74	/// [`Accumulator`]: crate::Accumulator
    75	/// [`create_udaf`]: crate::expr_fn::create_udaf
    76	/// [`simple_udaf.rs`]: https://github.com/apache/datafusion/blob/main/datafusion-examples/examples/simple_udaf.rs
    77	/// [`advanced_udaf.rs`]: https://github.com/apache/datafusion/blob/main/datafusion-examples/examples/advanced_udaf.rs
    78	#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialOrd)]
    79	pub struct AggregateUDF {
    80	    inner: Arc<dyn AggregateUDFImpl>,
    81	}
    82	
    83	impl PartialEq for AggregateUDF {
    84	    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
    85	        self.inner.equals(other.inner.as_ref())
    86	    }
    87	}
    88	
    89	impl Eq for AggregateUDF {}
    90	
    91	impl Hash for AggregateUDF {
    92	    fn hash<H: Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
    93	        self.inner.hash_value().hash(state)
    94	    }
    95	}
    96	
    97	impl fmt::Display for AggregateUDF {
    98	    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut Formatter) -> fmt::Result {
    99	        write!(f, "{}", self.name())
   100	    }
   101	}

   103	/// Arguments passed to [`AggregateUDFImpl::value_from_stats`]
   104	#[derive(Debug)]
   105	pub struct StatisticsArgs<'a> {
   106	    /// The statistics of the aggregate input
   107	    pub statistics: &'a Statistics,
   108	    /// The resolved return type of the aggregate function
   109	    pub return_type: &'a DataType,
   110	    /// Whether the aggregate function is distinct.
   111	    ///
   112	    /// ```sql
   113	    /// SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT column1) FROM t;
   114	    /// ```
   115	    pub is_distinct: bool,
   116	    /// The physical expression of arguments the aggregate function takes.
   117	    pub exprs: &'a [Arc<dyn PhysicalExpr>],
   118	}

   120	impl AggregateUDF {
   121	    /// Create a new `AggregateUDF` from a `[AggregateUDFImpl]` trait object
   122	    ///
   123	    /// Note this is the same as using the `From` impl (`AggregateUDF::from`)
   124	    pub fn new_from_impl<F>(fun: F) -> AggregateUDF
   125	    where
   126	        F: AggregateUDFImpl + 'static,
   127	    {
   128	        Self::new_from_shared_impl(Arc::new(fun))
   129	    }
   130	
   131	    /// Create a new `AggregateUDF` from a `[AggregateUDFImpl]` trait object
   132	    pub fn new_from_shared_impl(fun: Arc<dyn AggregateUDFImpl>) -> AggregateUDF {
   133	        Self { inner: fun }
   134	    }
   135	
   136	    /// Return the underlying [`AggregateUDFImpl`] trait object for this function
   137	    pub fn inner(&self) -> &Arc<dyn AggregateUDFImpl> {
   138	        &self.inner
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    /// Adds additional names that can be used to invoke this function, in
   142	    /// addition to `name`
   143	    ///
   144	    /// If you implement [`AggregateUDFImpl`] directly you should return aliases directly.
   145	    pub fn with_aliases(self, aliases: impl IntoIterator<Item = &'static str>) -> Self {
   146	        Self::new_from_impl(AliasedAggregateUDFImpl::new(
   147	            Arc::clone(&self.inner),
   148	            aliases,
   149	        ))
   150	    }
   151	
   152	    /// Creates an [`Expr`] that calls the aggregate function.
   153	    ///
   154	    /// This utility allows using the UDAF without requiring access to
   155	    /// the registry, such as with the DataFrame API.
   156	    pub fn call(&self, args: Vec<Expr>) -> Expr {
   157	        Expr::AggregateFunction(AggregateFunction::new_udf(
   158	            Arc::new(self.clone()),
   159	            args,
   160	            false,

   165	    }

   345	impl<F> From<F> for AggregateUDF
   346	where
   347	    F: AggregateUDFImpl + Send + Sync + 'static,
   348	{
   349	    fn from(fun: F) -> Self {
   350	        Self::new_from_impl(fun)
   351	    }

   354	/// Trait for implementing [`AggregateUDF`].
   355	///
   356	/// This trait exposes the full API for implementing user defined aggregate functions and
   357	/// can be used to implement any function.
   358	///
   359	/// See [`advanced_udaf.rs`] for a full example with complete implementation and
   360	/// [`AggregateUDF`] for other available options.
   361	///
   362	/// [`advanced_udaf.rs`]: https://github.com/apache/datafusion/blob/main/datafusion-examples/examples/advanced_udaf.rs
   363	///
   364	/// # Basic Example
   365	/// ```
   366	/// # use std::any::Any;
   367	/// # use std::sync::{Arc, LazyLock};
   368	/// # use arrow::datatypes::{DataType, FieldRef};
   369	/// # use datafusion_common::{DataFusionError, plan_err, Result};
   370	/// # use datafusion_expr::{col, ColumnarValue, Signature, Volatility, Expr, Documentation};
   371	/// # use datafusion_expr::{AggregateUDFImpl, AggregateUDF, Accumulator, function::{AccumulatorArgs, StateFieldsArgs}};
   372	/// # use datafusion_expr::window_doc_sections::DOC_SECTION_AGGREGATE;
   373	/// # use arrow::datatypes::Schema;
   374	/// # use arrow::datatypes::Field;
   375	///
   376	/// #[derive(Debug, Clone)]
   377	/// struct GeoMeanUdf {
   378	///   signature: Signature,
   379	/// }
   380	///
   381	/// impl GeoMeanUdf {
   382	///   fn new() -> Self {
   383	///     Self {
   384	///       signature: Signature::uniform(1, vec![DataType::Float64], Volatility::Immutable),
   385	///      }
   386	///   }
   387	/// }
   388	///
   389	/// static DOCUMENTATION: LazyLock<Documentation> = LazyLock::new(|| {
   390	///         Documentation::builder(DOC_SECTION_AGGREGATE, "calculates a geometric mean", "geo_mean(2.0)")
   391	///             .with_argument("arg1", "The Float64 number for the geometric mean")
   392	///             .build()
   393	///     });
   394	///
   395	/// fn get_doc() -> &'static Documentation {
   396	///     &DOCUMENTATION
   397	/// }
   398	///
   399	/// /// Implement the AggregateUDFImpl trait for GeoMeanUdf
   400	/// impl AggregateUDFImpl for GeoMeanUdf {
   401	///    fn as_any(&self) -> &dyn Any { self }
   402	///    fn name(&self) -> &str { "geo_mean" }
   403	///    fn signature(&self) -> &Signature { &self.signature }
   404	///    fn return_type(&self, args: &[DataType]) -> Result<DataType> {
   405	///      if !matches!(args.get(0), Some(&DataType::Float64)) {
   406	///        return plan_err!("geo_mean only accepts Float64 arguments");
   407	///      }
   408	///      Ok(DataType::Float64)
   409	///    }
   410	///    // This is the accumulator factory; DataFusion uses it to create new accumulators.
   411	///    fn accumulator(&self, _acc_args: AccumulatorArgs) -> Result<Box<dyn Accumulator>> { unimplemented!() }
   412	///    fn state_fields(&self, args: StateFieldsArgs) -> Result<Vec<FieldRef>> {
   413	///        Ok(vec![
   414	///             Arc::new(args.return_field.as_ref().clone().with_name("value")),
   415	///             Arc::new(Field::new("ordering", DataType::UInt32, true))
   416	///        ])
   417	///    }
   418	///    fn documentation(&self) -> Option<&Documentation> {
   419	///        Some(get_doc())
   420	///    }
   421	/// }
   422	///
   423	/// // Create a new AggregateUDF from the implementation
   424	/// let geometric_mean = AggregateUDF::from(GeoMeanUdf::new());
   425	///
   426	/// // Call the function `geo_mean(col)`
   427	/// let expr = geometric_mean.call(vec![col("a")]);
   428	/// ```
   429	pub trait AggregateUDFImpl: Debug + Send + Sync {
   430	    /// Returns this object as an [`Any`] trait object
   431	    fn as_any(&self) -> &dyn Any;
   432	
   433	    /// Returns this function's name
   434	    fn name(&self) -> &str;
   435	
   436	    /// Returns any aliases (alternate names) for this function.
   437	    ///
   438	    /// Note: `aliases` should only include names other than [`Self::name`].
   439	    /// Defaults to `[]` (no aliases)
   440	    fn aliases(&self) -> &[String] {
   441	        &[]
   442	    }
   443	
   444	    /// Returns the name of the column this expression would create
   445	    ///
   446	    /// See [`Expr::schema_name`] for details
   447	    ///
   448	    /// Example of schema_name: count(DISTINCT column1) <response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you.     18	use crate::{AggregateUDFImpl, ScalarUDFImpl, WindowUDFImpl};
    19	use std::fmt::Debug;
    20	use std::hash::{DefaultHasher, Hash, Hasher};
    21	use std::ops::Deref;
    22	use std::sync::Arc;
    23	
    24	/// A wrapper around a pointer to UDF that implements `Eq` and `Hash` delegating to
    25	/// corresponding methods on the UDF trait.
    26	///
    27	/// If you want to just compare pointers for equality, use [`super::ptr_eq::PtrEq`].
    28	#[derive(Clone)]
    29	#[allow(private_bounds)] // This is so that UdfEq can only be used with allowed pointer types (e.g. Arc), without allowing misuse.
    30	pub struct UdfEq<Ptr: UdfPointer>(Ptr);
    31	
    32	impl<Ptr> PartialEq for UdfEq<Ptr>
    33	where
    34	    Ptr: UdfPointer,
    35	{
    36	    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
    37	        self.0.equals(&other.0)
    38	    }
    39	}
    40	impl<Ptr> Eq for UdfEq<Ptr> where Ptr: UdfPointer {}
    41	impl<Ptr> Hash for UdfEq<Ptr>
    42	where
    43	    Ptr: UdfPointer,
    44	{
    45	    fn hash<H: Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
    46	        self.0.hash_value().hash(state);
    47	    }
    48	}
    49	
    50	impl<Ptr> From<Ptr> for UdfEq<Ptr>
    51	where
    52	    Ptr: UdfPointer,
    53	{
    54	    fn from(ptr: Ptr) -> Self {
    55	        UdfEq(ptr)
    56	    }
    57	}
    58	
    59	impl<Ptr> Debug for UdfEq<Ptr>
    60	where
    61	    Ptr: UdfPointer + Debug,
    62	{
    63	    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
    64	        self.0.fmt(f)
    65	    }
    66	}
    67	
    68	impl<Ptr> Deref for UdfEq<Ptr>
    69	where
    70	    Ptr: UdfPointer,
    71	{
    72	    type Target = Ptr;
    73	
    74	    fn deref(&self) -> &Self::Target {
    75	        &self.0
    76	    }
    77	}
    78	
    79	trait UdfPointer: Deref {
    80	    fn equals(&self, other: &Self::Target) -> bool;
    81	    fn hash_value(&self) -> u64;
    82	}
    83	
    84	macro_rules! impl_for_udf_eq {
    85	    ($udf:ty) => {
    86	        impl UdfPointer for Arc<$udf> {
    87	            fn equals(&self, other: &$udf) -> bool {
    88	                self.as_ref().equals(other)
    89	            }
    90	
    91	            fn hash_value(&self) -> u64 {
    92	                self.as_ref().hash_value()
    93	            }
    94	        }
    95	    };
    96	}
    97	
    98	impl_for_udf_eq!(dyn AggregateUDFImpl + '_);
    99	impl_for_udf_eq!(dyn ScalarUDFImpl + '_);
   100	
   101	impl UdfPointer for Arc<dyn WindowUDFImpl + '_> {
   102	    fn equals(&self, other: &(dyn WindowUDFImpl + '_)) -> bool {
   103	        self.as_ref().dyn_eq(other.as_any())
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    fn hash_value(&self) -> u64 {
   107	        let hasher = &mut DefaultHasher::new();
   108	        self.as_ref().dyn_hash(hasher);
   109	        hasher.finish()
   110	    }
   111	}

   156	    #[test]
   157	    pub fn test_eq_eq_wrapper() {
   158	        let signature = Signature::any(1, Volatility::Immutable);
   159	
   160	        let a1: Arc<dyn ScalarUDFImpl> = Arc::new(TestScalarUDF {
   161	            signature: signature.clone(),
   162	            name: "a",
   163	        });
   164	        let a2: Arc<dyn ScalarUDFImpl> = Arc::new(TestScalarUDF {
   165	            signature: signature.clone(),
   166	            name: "a",
   167	        });
   168	        let b: Arc<dyn ScalarUDFImpl> = Arc::new(TestScalarUDF {
   169	            signature: signature.clone(),
   170	            name: "b",
   171	        });
   172	
   173	        // Reflexivity
   174	        let wrapper = UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1));
   175	        assert_eq!(wrapper, wrapper);
   176	
   177	        // Two wrappers around equal pointer
   178	        assert_eq!(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1)), UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1)));
   179	        assert_eq!(hash(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1))), hash(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1))));
   180	
   181	        // Two wrappers around different pointers but equal in ScalarUDFImpl::equals sense
   182	        assert_eq!(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1)), UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a2)));
   183	        assert_eq!(hash(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1))), hash(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a2))));
   184	
   185	        // different functions (not equal)
   186	        assert_ne!(UdfEq(Arc::clone(&a1)), UdfEq(Arc::clone(&b)));
   187	    }
   188	
   189	    fn hash<T: Hash>(value: T) -> u64 {
   190	        let hasher = &mut DefaultHasher::new();
   191	        value.hash(hasher);
   192	        hasher.finish()
   193	    }
   194	}

   920	    /// *Must* be implemented explicitly if the UDF type has internal state.
   921	    /// Must be consistent with [`Self::hash_value`] and follow the same rules as [`Eq`]:
   922	    ///
   923	    /// - reflexive: `a.equals(a)`;
   924	    /// - symmetric: `a.equals(b)` implies `b.equals(a)`;
   925	    /// - transitive: `a.equals(b)` and `b.equals(c)` implies `a.equals(c)`.
   926	    ///
   927	    /// By default, compares type, [`Self::name`], [`Self::aliases`] and [`Self::signature`].
   928	    fn equals(&self, other: &dyn AggregateUDFImpl) -> bool {
   929	        self.as_any().type_id() == other.as_any().type_id()
   930	            && self.name() == other.name()
   931	            && self.aliases() == other.aliases()
   932	            && self.signature() == other.signature()
   933	    }
   934	
   935	    /// Returns a hash value for this aggregate UDF.
   936	    ///
   937	    /// Allows customizing the hash code of aggregate UDFs.
   938	    /// *Must* be implemented explicitly whenever [`Self::equals`] is implemented.
   939	    ///
   940	    /// Similarly to [`Hash`] and [`Eq`], if [`Self::equals`] returns true for two UDFs,
   941	    /// their `hash_value`s must be the same.
   942	    ///
   943	    /// By default, it only hashes the type. The other fields are not hashed, as usually the
   944	    /// name, signature, and aliases are implied by the UDF type. Recall that UDFs with state
   945	    /// (and thus possibly changing fields) must override [`Self::equals`] and [`Self::hash_value`].
   946	    fn hash_value(&self) -> u64 {
   947	        let hasher = &mut DefaultHasher::new();
   948	        self.as_any().type_id().hash(hasher);
   949	        hasher.finish()
   950	    }
   951	
   952	    /// If this function is max, return true
   953	    /// If the function is min, return false
   954	    /// Otherwise return None (the default)
   955	    ///
   956	    ///
   957	    /// Note: this is used to use special aggregate implementations in certain conditions
   958	    fn is_descending(&self) -> Option<bool> {
   959	        None
   960	    }
   961	
   962	    /// Return the value of this aggregate function if it can be determined
   963	    /// entirely from statistics and arguments.
   964	    ///
   965	    /// Using a [`ScalarValue`] rather than a runtime computation can significantly
   966	    /// improving query performance.
   967	    ///
   968	    /// For example, if the minimum value of column `x` is known to be `42` from
   969	    /// statistics, then the aggregate `MIN(x)` should return `Some(ScalarValue(42))`
   970	    fn value_from_stats(&self, _statistics_args: &StatisticsArgs) -> Option<ScalarValue> {

    72	    Expr::AggregateFunction(datafusion_expr::expr::AggregateFunction::new_udf(
    73	        count_udaf(),

    78	        None,

    80	}

    82	/// Creates aggregation to count all rows.
    83	///
    84	/// In SQL this is `SELECT COUNT(*) ... `
    85	///
    86	/// The expression is equivalent to `COUNT(*)`, `COUNT()`, `COUNT(1)`, and is
    87	/// aliased to a column named `"count(*)"` for backward compatibility.
    88	///
    89	/// Example
    90	/// ```
    91	/// # use datafusion_functions_aggregate::count::count_all;
    92	/// # use datafusion_expr::col;
    93	/// // create `count(*)` expression
    94	/// let expr = count_all();
    95	/// assert_eq!(expr.schema_name().to_string(), "count(*)");
    96	/// // if you need to refer to this column, use the `schema_name` function
    97	/// let expr = col(expr.schema_name().to_string());
    98	/// ```
    99	pub fn count_all() -> Expr {
   100	    count(Expr::Literal(COUNT_STAR_EXPANSION, None)).alias("count(*)")

   284	    }

   302	    fn state_fields(&self, args: StateFieldsArgs) -> Result<Vec<FieldRef>> {
   303	        if args.is_distinct {
   304	            let dtype: DataType = match &args.input_fields[0].data_type() {
   305	                DataType::Dictionary(_, values_type) => (**values_type).clone(),
   306	                &dtype => dtype.clone(),
   307	            };
   308	
   309	            Ok(vec![Field::new_list(
   310	                format_state_name(args.name, "count distinct"),
   311	                // See COMMENTS.md to understand why nullable is set to true
   312	                Field::new_list_field(dtype, true),
   313	                false,
   314	            )
   315	            .into()])
   316	        } else {
   317	            Ok(vec![Field::new(
   318	                format_state_name(args.name, "count"),
   319	                DataType::Int64,
   320	                false,
   321	            )
   322	            .into()])
   323	        }
   324	    }
   325	
   326	    fn accumulator(&self, acc_args: AccumulatorArgs) -> Result<Box<dyn Accumulator>> {
   327	        if !acc_args.is_distinct {
   328	            return Ok(Box::new(CountAccumulator::new()));
   329	        }
   330	
   331	        if acc_args.exprs.len() > 1 {
   332	            return not_impl_err!("COUNT DISTINCT with multiple arguments");
   333	        }
   334	
   335	        let data_type = &acc_args.exprs[0].data_type(acc_args.schema)?;
   336	
   337	        Ok(match data_type {
   338	            DataType::Dictionary(_, values_type) => {
   339	                let inner = get_count_accumulator(values_type);
   340	                Box::new(DictionaryCountAccumulator::new(inner))
   341	            }
   342	            _ => get_count_accumulator(data_type),
   343	        })
   344	    }
   345	
   346	    fn groups_accumulator_supported(&self, args: AccumulatorArgs) -> bool {
   347	        // groups accumulator only supports `COUNT(c1)`, not
   348	        // `COUNT(c1, c2)`, etc
   349	        if args.is_distinct {
   350	            return false;

   374	        }

   393	                        return Some(ScalarValue::Int64(Some(num_rows as i64)));
   394	                    }
   395	                }
   396	            }
   397	        }

    18	//! [`ScalarUDF`]: Scalar User Defined Functions
    19	
    20	use crate::async_udf::AsyncScalarUDF;
    21	use crate::expr::schema_name_from_exprs_comma_separated_without_space;
    22	use crate::simplify::{ExprSimplifyResult, SimplifyInfo};
    23	use crate::sort_properties::{ExprProperties, SortProperties};

    25	use crate::{udf_equals_hash, ColumnarValue, Documentation, Expr, Signature};
    26	use arrow::datatypes::{DataType, Field, FieldRef};
    27	use datafusion_common::config::ConfigOptions;
    28	use datafusion_common::{not_impl_err, ExprSchema, Result, ScalarValue};
    29	use datafusion_expr_common::interval_arithmetic::Interval;
    30	use std::any::Any;
    31	use std::cmp::Ordering;
    32	use std::fmt::Debug;
    33	use std::hash::{DefaultHasher, Hash, Hasher};
    34	use std::sync::Arc;
    35	
    36	/// Logical representation of a Scalar User Defined Function.
    37	///
    38	/// A scalar function produces a single row output for each row of input. This
    39	/// struct contains the information DataFusion needs to plan and invoke
    40	/// functions you supply such as name, type signature, return type, and actual
    41	/// implementation.
    42	///
    43	/// 1. For simple use cases, use [`create_udf`] (examples in [`simple_udf.rs`]).
    44	///
    45	/// 2. For advanced use cases, use [`ScalarUDFImpl`] which provides full API
    46	///    access (examples in  [`advanced_udf.rs`]).
    47	///
    48	/// See [`Self::call`] to create an `Expr` which invokes a `ScalarUDF` with arguments.
    49	///
    50	/// # API Note
    51	///
    52	/// This is a separate struct from [`ScalarUDFImpl`] to maintain backwards
    53	/// compatibility with the older API.
    54	///
    55	/// [`create_udf`]: crate::expr_fn::create_udf
    56	/// [`simple_udf.rs`]: https://github.com/apache/datafusion/blob/main/datafusion-examples/examples/simple_udf.rs
    57	/// [`advanced_udf.rs`]: https://github.com/apache/datafusion/blob/main/datafusion-examples/examples/advanced_udf.rs
    58	#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
    59	pub struct ScalarUDF {
    60	    inner: Arc<dyn ScalarUDFImpl>,
    61	}
    62	
    63	impl PartialEq for ScalarUDF {
    64	    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
    65	        self.inner.equals(other.inner.as_ref())
    66	    }
    67	}
    68	
    69	// Manual implementation based on `ScalarUDFImpl::equals`
    70	impl PartialOrd for ScalarUDF {
    71	    fn partial_cmp(&self, other: &Self) -> Option<Ordering> {
    72	        match self.name().partial_cmp(other.name()) {
    73	            Some(Ordering::Equal) => self.signature().partial_cmp(other.signature()),
    74	            cmp => cmp,
    75	        }
    76	    }
    77	}
    78	
    79	impl Eq for ScalarUDF {}
    80	
    81	impl Hash for ScalarUDF {
    82	    fn hash<H: Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
    83	        self.inner.hash_value().hash(state)
    84	    }
    85	}
    86	
    87	impl ScalarUDF {
    88	    /// Create a new `ScalarUDF` from a `[ScalarUDFImpl]` trait object
    89	    ///
    90	    /// Note this is the same as using the `From` impl (`ScalarUDF::from`)
    91	    pub fn new_from_impl<F>(fun: F) -> ScalarUDF
    92	    where
    93	        F: ScalarUDFImpl + 'static,
    94	    {
    95	        Self::new_from_shared_impl(Arc::new(fun))
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    /// Create a new `ScalarUDF` from a `[ScalarUDFImpl]` trait object
    99	    pub fn new_from_shared_impl(fun: Arc<dyn ScalarUDFImpl>) -> ScalarUDF {
   100	        Self { inner: fun }

   700	    ///
   701	    /// Allows customizing the equality of scalar UDFs.
   702	    /// *Must* be implemented explicitly if the UDF type has internal state.
   703	    /// Must be consistent with [`Self::hash_value`] and follow the same rules as [`Eq`]:
   704	    ///
   705	    /// - reflexive: `a.equals(a)`;
   706	    /// - symmetric: `a.equals(b)` implies `b.equals(a)`;
   707	    /// - transitive: `a.equals(b)` and `b.equals(c)` implies `a.equals(c)`.
   708	    ///
   709	    /// By default, compares type, [`Self::name`], [`Self::aliases`] and [`Self::signature`].
   710	    fn equals(&self, other: &dyn ScalarUDFImpl) -> bool {
   711	        self.as_any().type_id() == other.as_any().type_id()
   712	            && self.name() == other.name()
   713	            && self.aliases() == other.aliases()
   714	            && self.signature() == other.signature()
   715	    }
   716	
   717	    /// Returns a hash value for this scalar UDF.
   718	    ///
   719	    /// Allows customizing the hash code of scalar UDFs.
   720	    /// *Must* be implemented explicitly whenever [`Self::equals`] is implemented.
   721	    ///
   722	    /// Similarly to [`Hash`] and [`Eq`], if [`Self::equals`] returns true for two UDFs,
   723	    /// their `hash_value`s must be the same.
   724	    ///
   725	    /// By default, it only hashes the type. The other fields are not hashed, as usually the
   726	    /// name, signature, and aliases are implied by the UDF type. Recall that UDFs with state
   727	    /// (and thus possibly changing fields) must override [`Self::equals`] and [`Self::hash_value`].
   728	    fn hash_value(&self) -> u64 {
   729	        let hasher = &mut DefaultHasher::new();
   730	        self.as_any().type_id().hash(hasher);
   731	        hasher.finish()
   732	    }
   733	
   734	    /// Returns the documentation for this Scalar UDF.
   735	    ///
   736	    /// Documentation can be accessed programmatically as well as generating
   737	    /// publicly facing documentation.
   738	    fn documentation(&self) -> Option<&Documentation> {
   739	        None
   740	    }
   741	}

   744	/// implement [`ScalarUDFImpl`], which supports aliases, directly if possible.
   745	#[derive(Debug, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
   746	struct AliasedScalarUDFImpl {

    17	
    18	use std::any::Any;
    19	use std::hash::{Hash, Hasher};
    20	
    21	/// A dyn-compatible version of [`Eq`] trait.
    22	/// The implementation constraints for this trait are the same as for [`Eq`]:
    23	/// the implementation must be reflexive, symmetric, and transitive.
    24	/// Additionally, if two values can be compared with [`DynEq`] and [`PartialEq`] then
    25	/// they must be [`DynEq`]-equal if and only if they are [`PartialEq`]-equal.
    26	/// It is therefore strongly discouraged to implement this trait for types
    27	/// that implement `PartialEq<Other>` or `Eq<Other>` for any type `Other` other than `Self`.
    28	///
    29	/// Note: This trait should not be implemented directly. Implement `Eq` and `Any` and use
    30	/// the blanket implementation.
    31	#[allow(private_bounds)]
    32	pub trait DynEq: private::EqSealed {
    33	    fn dyn_eq(&self, other: &dyn Any) -> bool;
    34	}
    35	
    36	impl<T: Eq + Any> private::EqSealed for T {}
    37	impl<T: Eq + Any> DynEq for T {
    38	    fn dyn_eq(&self, other: &dyn Any) -> bool {
    39	        other.downcast_ref::<Self>() == Some(self)
    40	    }
    41	}
    42	
    43	/// A dyn-compatible version of [`Hash`] trait.
    44	/// If two values are equal according to [`DynEq`], they must produce the same hash value.
    45	///
    46	/// Note: This trait should not be implemented directly. Implement `Hash` and `Any` and use
    47	/// the blanket implementation.
    48	#[allow(private_bounds)]
    49	pub trait DynHash: private::HashSealed {
    50	    fn dyn_hash(&self, _state: &mut dyn Hasher);
    51	}
    52	
    53	impl<T: Hash + Any> private::HashSealed for T {}
    54	impl<T: Hash + Any> DynHash for T {
    55	    fn dyn_hash(&self, mut state: &mut dyn Hasher) {
    56	        self.type_id().hash(&mut state);
    57	        self.hash(&mut state)
    58	    }
    59	}
    60	
    61	mod private {
    62	    pub(super) trait EqSealed {}
    63	    pub(super) trait HashSealed {}
    64	}
    65

   911	    /// A Vec the same length as `arg_types`. DataFusion will `CAST` the function call
   912	    /// arguments to these specific types.
   913	    fn coerce_types(&self, _arg_types: &[DataType]) -> Result<Vec<DataType>> {
   914	        not_impl_err!("Function {} does not implement coerce_types", self.name())
   915	    }
   916	
   917	    /// Return true if this aggregate UDF is equal to the other.
   918	    ///
   919	    /// Allows customizing the equality of aggregate UDFs.
   920	    /// *Must* be implemented explicitly if the UDF type has internal state.
   921	    /// Must be consistent with [`Self::hash_value`] and follow the same rules as [`Eq`]:
   922	    ///
   923	    /// - reflexive: `a.equals(a)`;
   924	    /// - symmetric: `a.equals(b)` implies `b.equals(a)`;
   925	    /// - transitive: `a.equals(b)` and `b.equals(c)` implies `a.equals(c)`.
   926	    ///
   927	    /// By default, compares type, [`Self::name`], [`Self::aliases`] and [`Self::signature`].
   928	    fn equals(&self, other: &dyn AggregateUDFImpl) -> bool {
   929	        self.as_any().type_id() == other.as_any().type_id()
   930	            && self.name() == other.name()
   931	            && self.aliases() == other.aliases()
   932	            && self.signature() == other.signature()
   933	    }
   934	
   935	    /// Returns a hash value for this aggregate UDF.
   936	    ///
   937	    /// Allows customizing the hash code of aggregate UDFs.
   938	    /// *Must* be implemented explicitly whenever [`Self::equals`] is implemented.
   939	    ///
   940	    /// Similarly to [`Hash`] and [`Eq`], if [`Self::equals`] returns true for two UDFs,
   941	    /// their `hash_value`s must be the same.
   942	    ///
   943	    /// By default, it only hashes the type. The other fields are not hashed, as usually the
   944	    /// name, signature, and aliases are implied by the UDF type. Recall that UDFs with state
   945	    /// (and thus possibly changing fields) must override [`Self::equals`] and [`Self::hash_value`].
   946	    fn hash_value(&self) -> u64 {
   947	        let hasher = &mut DefaultHasher::new();
   948	        self.as_any().type_id().hash(hasher);
   949	        hasher.finish()
   950	    }
   951

   953	    /// If the function is min, return false

   959	        None

    /// Return true if this aggregate UDF is equal to the other.
    ///
    /// Allows customizing the equality of aggregate UDFs.
    /// *Must* be implemented explicitly if the UDF type has internal state.
    /// Must be consistent with [`Self::hash_value`] and follow the same rules as [`Eq`]:
    ///
    /// - reflexive: `a.equals(a)`;
    /// - symmetric: `a.equals(b)` implies `b.equals(a)`;
    /// - transitive: `a.equals(b)` and `b.equals(c)` implies `a.equals(c)`.
    ///
    /// By default, compares type, [`Self::name`], [`Self::aliases`] and [`Self::signature`].
    fn equals(&self, other: &dyn AggregateUDFImpl) -> bool {
        self.as_any().type_id() == other.as_any().type_id()
            && self.name() == other.name()
            && self.aliases() == other.aliases()
            && self.signature() == other.signature()
    }

    /// Returns a hash value for this aggregate UDF.
    ///
    /// Allows customizing the hash code of aggregate UDFs.
    /// *Must* be implemented explicitly whenever [`Self::equals`] is implemented.
    ///
    /// Similarly to [`Hash`] and [`Eq`], if [`Self::equals`] returns true for two UDFs,
    /// their `hash_value`s must be the same.
    ///
    /// By default, it only hashes the type. The other fields are not hashed, as usually the
    /// name, signature, and aliases are implied by the UDF type. Recall that UDFs with state
    /// (and thus possibly changing fields) must override [`Self::equals`] and [`Self::hash_value`].
    fn hash_value(&self) -> u64 {
        let hasher = &mut DefaultHasher::new();
        self.as_any().type_id().hash(hasher);
        hasher.finish()
    }

    /// If this function is max, return true

/// Example showing generation of [`ScalarUDFImpl::equals`] and [`ScalarUDFImpl::hash_value`]
/// implementations.
///
/// ```
/// # use arrow::datatypes::DataType;
/// # use datafusion_expr::{udf_equals_hash, ScalarFunctionArgs, ScalarUDFImpl};
/// # use datafusion_expr_common::columnar_value::ColumnarValue;
/// # use datafusion_expr_common::signature::Signature;
/// # use std::any::Any;
///
/// // Implementing Eq & Hash is a prerequisite for using this macro,
/// // but the implementation can be derived.
/// #[derive(Debug, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
/// struct VarcharToTimestampTz {
///     safe: bool,
/// }
///
/// impl ScalarUDFImpl for VarcharToTimestampTz {
///     /* other methods omitted for brevity */
/// #    fn as_any(&self) -> &dyn Any {
/// #        self
/// #    }
/// #
/// #    fn name(&self) -> &str {
/// #        "varchar_to_timestamp_tz"
/// #    }
--
/// #        args: ScalarFunctionArgs,
/// #    ) -> datafusion_common::Result<ColumnarValue> {
/// #        todo!()
/// #    }
/// #
///     udf_equals_hash!(ScalarUDFImpl);
/// }
/// ```
///
/// [`ScalarUDFImpl::equals`]: crate::ScalarUDFImpl::equals
/// [`ScalarUDFImpl::hash_value`]: crate::ScalarUDFImpl::hash_value
#[macro_export]
macro_rules! udf_equals_hash {
    ($udf_type:tt) => {
        fn equals(&self, other: &dyn $udf_type) -> bool {
            use ::core::any::Any;
            use ::core::cmp::{Eq, PartialEq};
            let Some(other) = <dyn Any + 'static>::downcast_ref::<Self>(other.as_any())
            else {
                return false;
            };
            fn assert_self_impls_eq<T: Eq>() {}
            assert_self_impls_eq::<Self>();
            PartialEq::eq(self, other)
        }

        fn hash_value(&self) -> u64 {
            use ::std::any::type_name;
            use ::std::hash::{DefaultHasher, Hash, Hasher};
            let hasher = &mut DefaultHasher::new();
            type_name::<Self>().hash(hasher);
            Hash::hash(self, hasher);
            Hasher::finish(hasher)
